-- HOW TO USE THIS REPORT --

"Optional Views for Improved Readability

The large amount of information in the Court Report can make it difficult to fit all information on a printed page and still keep the font at a size that is easy to read.  To assist in making the printed report easier to read and therefore easier to use in court we have used Excels Group feature to allow the person reviewing and/or printing the report to collapse view of the less significant information columns of Agency Name and Officer Name.  The user can decide the importance of including or excluding these columns in the printed report."
"Raw CourtReport  tab

All text in the Notes column is visible when viewing from the computer screen.  However on the printed page the text is truncated to accommodate limitations of page width.  The full and complete text for Notes can be viewed and printed from the Alarm Actions tab of the Court Report."
